# Review of M5 (Push + delivery + dynamic notifications)

The build is now in the "Claude builds, others review" protocol (lead switched from Codex after Codex hit usage limit). I (Claude) just authored M5 across two commits:

- `927359c` M5 (server): push delivery + messages + senders endpoints
- `f29c3ba` M5 (android): :core:push module - FCM service + foreground service

Review focus: security, contract adherence, edge cases. Items I want pressure-tested below.

## What landed

**Server (`server/`):**
- `app/services/senders.py` — register/get/get_active/revoke
- `app/services/messages.py` — store_message (validates pairing, plugin, devices; 410 if none), inbox_for_device, get_message_for_user, mark_dismissed; encrypted_body_pointer "inline:" scheme
- `app/services/push.py` — Firebase Admin lazy init; dev-mode no-op; FCM data payload contains ONLY (type, message_id, plugin_id, min_plugin_version) — never plaintext
- `app/routers/senders.py` — POST /v1/senders/register (rate-limited like signup)
- `app/routers/messages.py` — POST /send (sender-signed envelope verified via Ed25519), GET /inbox, GET /{id}, POST /{id}/dismiss
- `app/main.py`, `app/config.py`, `app/schemas.py`, `.env.example`, `pyproject.toml` updates
- `tests/test_messages.py` — happy path + 401 bad-sig + 410 no-device + dismiss

**Android (`android/core/push/`):**
- `SynclerFcmService` (FirebaseMessagingService) — routes data["type"] to PluginNotificationService or DismissEventHandler
- `PluginNotificationService` (Foreground Service, dataSync type on API 34+) — fetches body, decrypts, dispatches to PluginRegistry, builds final user notification
- `BatteryOptimizationCheck` — directs user to disable optimization for the app
- `PluginMessagePipeline` interface (host app implements)
- `FcmDispatcher`, `FcmTokenRegistrar` interfaces (host app implements)
- `DefaultNotificationFactory` + Hilt module
- Updated `core/network/SynclerApi.kt` with getMessage, inbox, dismissMessage endpoints
- AndroidManifest: declares both services with proper permissions

## Things I want you to pressure-test

1. **Envelope canonical bytes.** `routers/messages.py` builds `envelope_bytes` from `{sender_id, user_id, plugin_id, encrypted_body, nonce, min_plugin_version}` with sort_keys + separators(",", ":"). Sender SDK (not yet written — M9) MUST produce byte-identical bytes when signing. Is the field set complete? Should `expires_at` or a server-generated `message_id` be in the AAD/envelope? Trade-off: more fields = more replay protection, fewer fields = sender doesn't need to predict server state.

2. **AAD vs envelope.** The crypto-spec defines AAD = (message_id, sender_id, user_id, plugin_id, min_plugin_version, created_at, schema_version). But message_id is server-generated AFTER the sender signs. How does the sender include message_id in AAD if they don't know it yet? Either the AAD must be relaxed for V1 OR the sender generates a client-side message_id and the server adopts it. Currently the schema_version + created_at + message_id fields are likely DROPPED in my impl. Check.

3. **Replay window on /send.** Server doesn't dedupe by anything sender-supplied (e.g., idempotency_key). A network adversary intercepting one message can replay it. Server's `NonceRegistry` (M2) is in-memory only; tests use a fresh process. Real impact = duplicate delivery (plugin handles). Confirmed acceptable per Round 11 fix-up notes?

4. **encrypted_body_pointer inline scheme.** Stored as `inline:<b64_nonce>|<b64_ct>|<b64_sig>` in a TEXT column. Server parses it on inbox/fetch. Is the parsing robust? What if a malicious actor manages to register a sender and POST a body with the literal `|` separator in their base64 — wait, base64 doesn't include `|`. OK safe.

5. **Push payload leak surface.** Confirm I never include plaintext content in FCM data payload. Search `services/push.py` for plaintext leakage paths.

6. **Foreground service uptime budget.** PluginNotificationService has MAX_WORK_MS = 30s. If plugin code hangs, service aborts and user gets nothing. Is 30s the right number? Should this surface a "delivery failed" notification on timeout?

7. **Notification channel design.** Two channels: `syncler.foreground.delivery` (IMPORTANCE_MIN) and `syncler.user.messages` (IMPORTANCE_DEFAULT). User can disable either independently. Is this the right separation?

8. **Battery optimization UX.** `BatteryOptimizationCheck.requestIgnoreIntent` opens system settings. The Android manifest doesn't declare the related permission (`REQUEST_IGNORE_BATTERY_OPTIMIZATIONS`) — Play Store has policy restrictions on apps that request this. Is the helper enough for V1 (where user is dev) or does it need policy doc?

9. **POST /send rate limit by sender_id from header X-Sender-ID.** Header is unauthenticated input before signature verification. A spammer could send a flood of requests with random X-Sender-ID values bypassing the per-sender bucket. Counter-argument: each request still has to hit signature verification which is CPU-bound, but the bucket itself can be flooded. Is this OK for V1 or do we move to IP rate limit?

10. **Dismiss endpoint authn.** Currently JWT-auth via `current_user` and `device_id` is a query param (not validated to belong to the user). A user could dismiss messages by spoofing another device's device_id. Severity: own-account scope only. Should we add `device_id IN user's devices` check?


52:def _b64(value: bytes) -> str:
53:    return base64.b64encode(value).decode("ascii")

56:def _build_envelope_bytes(payload: MessageSendRequest) -> bytes:
57:    """Canonical envelope bytes for signature verification.
58:
59:    The sender signs the JSON of the envelope WITHOUT the signature field,
60:    with sorted keys and compact separators. Server reconstructs the same
61:    bytes for verification.
62:    """
63:    envelope = {
64:        "sender_id": str(payload.sender_id),
65:        "user_id": str(payload.user_id),
66:        "plugin_id": str(payload.plugin_id),
67:        "encrypted_body": payload.encrypted_body,
68:        "nonce": payload.nonce,
69:        "min_plugin_version": payload.min_plugin_version or "",
70:    }
71:    return json.dumps(envelope, sort_keys=True, separators=(",", ":")).encode("utf-8")

94:        message = await store_message(
95:            db,

1:"""Push delivery via Firebase Cloud Messaging (FCM).
2:
3:The platform is content-blind: the FCM payload contains only opaque metadata
4:(``message_id``, ``plugin_id``, ``min_plugin_version``). The device wakes,
5:fetches the encrypted body via ``GET /v1/messages/{id}``, decrypts locally,
6:and asks the plugin to render the notification.
7:
8:The Firebase Admin SDK is initialized lazily on first ``push_to_devices``
9:call. If ``FIREBASE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_PATH`` is unset the module operates in
10:no-op development mode and logs delivery intent.
11:"""
12:
13:from __future__ import annotations
14:
15:import logging
16:import uuid
17:from dataclasses import dataclass
18:from datetime import UTC, datetime
19:from typing import Any
20:
21:from sqlalchemy import select
22:from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession
23:
24:from app.config import Settings, get_settings
25:from app.models import DeliveryStatus, Device, Message
26:
27:logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
28:
29:_firebase_app: Any | None = None
30:_initialized = False
31:
32:
33:@dataclass
34:class FcmResult:
35:    device_id: uuid.UUID
36:    delivered: bool
37:    error: str | None = None
38:
39:
40:def _ensure_firebase(settings: Settings) -> Any | None:
41:    """Lazy-initialize the Firebase Admin app.
42:
43:    Returns the firebase app (or None in dev mode). Never raises on missing
44:    creds — instead degrades to dev-mode logging so local dev works without
45:    a Firebase project.
46:    """
47:    global _firebase_app, _initialized
48:    if _initialized:
49:        return _firebase_app
50:
51:    _initialized = True
52:    if not settings.firebase_service_account_path:
53:        logger.info("FCM not configured; running in dev-mode no-op")
54:        return None
55:
56:    try:
57:        import firebase_admin
58:        from firebase_admin import credentials
59:
60:        cred = credentials.Certificate(settings.firebase_service_account_path)
61:        _firebase_app = firebase_admin.initialize_app(cred)
62:        return _firebase_app
63:    except Exception as exc:
64:        logger.warning("failed to initialize Firebase Admin: %s", exc)
65:        return None
66:
67:
68:async def push_message_to_user_devices(
69:    db: AsyncSession,
70:    *,
71:    message: Message,
72:    settings: Settings | None = None,
73:) -> list[FcmResult]:
74:    """Fan out a freshly-stored message to each device's FCM token."""
75:    settings = settings or get_settings()
76:    app = _ensure_firebase(settings)
77:
78:    result = await db.execute(
79:        select(Device).where(
80:            Device.user_id == message.user_id,
81:            Device.revoked_at.is_(None),
82:            Device.fcm_token.is_not(None),
83:        ),
84:    )
85:    devices = list(result.scalars().all())
86:    if not devices:
87:        return []
88:
89:    payload = {
90:        "type": "message",
91:        "message_id": str(message.id),
92:        "plugin_id": str(message.plugin_id),
93:        "min_plugin_version": message.min_plugin_version or "",
94:    }
95:
96:    outcomes: list[FcmResult] = []
97:    for device in devices:
98:        outcome = _deliver(app, device, payload)
99:        outcomes.append(outcome)
100:        if not outcome.delivered and outcome.error == "invalid_token":
101:            device.fcm_token = None
102:
103:    # Record delivery timestamps for those that succeeded
104:    if any(o.delivered for o in outcomes):
105:        delivered_at = datetime.now(UTC)
106:        result = await db.execute(
107:            select(DeliveryStatus).where(DeliveryStatus.message_id == message.id),
108:        )
109:        delivery_rows = {row.device_id: row for row in result.scalars().all()}
110:        for outcome in outcomes:
111:            if outcome.delivered and outcome.device_id in delivery_rows:
112:                delivery_rows[outcome.device_id].delivered_at = delivered_at
113:
114:    await db.commit()
115:    return outcomes
116:
117:
118:async def push_dismiss_to_other_devices(
119:    db: AsyncSession,
120:    *,
121:    message: Message,
122:    dismissing_device_id: uuid.UUID,
123:    settings: Settings | None = None,
124:) -> list[FcmResult]:
125:    """Fan out a dismiss event to other devices when plugin behavior == DISMISS_ALL."""
126:    settings = settings or get_settings()
127:    app = _ensure_firebase(settings)
128:
129:    result = await db.execute(
130:        select(Device).where(
131:            Device.user_id == message.user_id,
132:            Device.id != dismissing_device_id,
133:            Device.revoked_at.is_(None),
134:            Device.fcm_token.is_not(None),
135:        ),
136:    )
137:    devices = list(result.scalars().all())
138:    if not devices:
139:        return []
140:
141:    payload = {
142:        "type": "dismiss",

153:            "FCM[dev] would deliver to device=%s payload=%s", device.id, payload
154:        )

158:        from firebase_admin import messaging
159:
160:        message = messaging.Message(
161:            data={k: str(v) for k, v in payload.items()},
162:            token=device.fcm_token,
163:            android=messaging.AndroidConfig(priority="high"),
164:        )
165:        messaging.send(message, app=app)
166:        return FcmResult(device_id=device.id, delivered=True)
167:    except Exception as exc:
168:        logger.warning("FCM delivery failed for device=%s: %s", device.id, exc)
169:        is_invalid = "registration-token-not-registered" in str(exc).lower() or "invalid-argument" in str(exc).lower()

171:            device_id=device.id,

17:def decode_base64(value: str, *, field_name: str, exact: int | None = None, minimum: int | None = None) -> bytes:
18:    try:
19:        decoded = base64.b64decode(value, validate=True)
20:    except (binascii.Error, ValueError) as exc:
21:        raise ValueError(f"{field_name} must be valid base64") from exc
22:
23:    if exact is not None and len(decoded) != exact:
24:        raise ValueError(f"{field_name} must decode to {exact} bytes")
25:    if minimum is not None and len(decoded) < minimum:
26:        raise ValueError(f"{field_name} must decode to at least {minimum} bytes")
27:
28:    return decoded

182:def _build_pointer(encrypted_body: bytes, nonce: bytes, envelope_signature: bytes) -> str:
183:    """Build the encrypted_body_pointer column value.
184:
185:    V1 stores the ciphertext inline as base64 segments separated by ``|`` so the
186:    server never decodes it and never sees plaintext. A future migration may
187:    move this to blob storage; the column type stays ``TEXT``.
188:    """
189:    import base64
190:
191:    encoded = base64.b64encode(encrypted_body).decode("ascii")
192:    nonce_encoded = base64.b64encode(nonce).decode("ascii")
193:    sig_encoded = base64.b64encode(envelope_signature).decode("ascii")
194:    return f"inline:{nonce_encoded}|{encoded}|{sig_encoded}"
195:
196:
197:def parse_pointer(pointer: str) -> tuple[bytes, bytes, bytes]:
198:    """Inverse of :func:`_build_pointer`."""
199:    import base64
200:
201:    if not pointer.startswith("inline:"):
202:        raise ValueError("unsupported pointer scheme")
203:    body = pointer[len("inline:") :]
204:    parts = body.split("|")
205:    if len(parts) != 3:
206:        raise ValueError("malformed pointer")
207:    nonce = base64.b64decode(parts[0])
208:    encrypted_body = base64.b64decode(parts[1])
209:    envelope_signature = base64.b64decode(parts[2])
210:    return encrypted_body, nonce, envelope_signature

14:def rate_limit(name: str) -> Callable[[Request, AsyncSession], Awaitable[None]]:
15:    config = RATE_LIMITS[name]
16:
17:    async def dependency(request: Request, db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)) -> None:
18:        await check_rate_limit(db, request, config)
19:
20:    return dependency

22:
23:async def check_rate_limit(db: AsyncSession, request: Request, config: RateLimitConfig) -> None:
24:    now = datetime.now(UTC)
25:    window_epoch = int(now.timestamp()) // config.window_seconds * config.window_seconds
26:    window_start = datetime.fromtimestamp(window_epoch, UTC)
27:    actor_type, actor_id = _identify_actor(config.name, request)
28:
29:    count = await _increment_and_read(
30:        db,
31:        actor_type=actor_type,
32:        actor_id=actor_id,
33:        route=config.name,
34:        window_start=window_start,
35:    )
36:    await db.commit()
37:
38:    if count > config.max_count:
39:        retry_after = max(1, ceil(window_epoch + config.window_seconds - now.timestamp()))
40:        raise HTTPException(
41:            status_code=status.HTTP_429_TOO_MANY_REQUESTS,
42:            detail="rate limited",
43:            headers={"Retry-After": str(retry_after)},
44:        )

68:            INSERT INTO rate_limit_events (actor_type, actor_id, route, window_start, count)
69:            VALUES (:actor_type, :actor_id, :route, :window_start, 1)
70:            ON CONFLICT (actor_type, actor_id, route, window_start)
71:            DO UPDATE SET count = rate_limit_events.count + 1
72:            RETURNING count
73:            """
74:        ),
75:        {
76:            "actor_type": actor_type,
77:            "actor_id": actor_id,

85:async def _increment_and_read_sqlite(
86:    db: AsyncSession,
87:    *,

89:    actor_id: str,
90:    route: str,
91:    window_start: datetime,

96:            SELECT id, count

107:            "route": route,

117:            {"count": next_count, "id": row_data["id"]},

122:    await db.execute(
123:        text(
124:            """
125:            INSERT INTO rate_limit_events (id, actor_type, actor_id, route, window_start, count)
126:            VALUES (:id, :actor_type, :actor_id, :route, :window_start, 1)
127:            """
128:        ),
129:        {
130:            "id": int(max_id.scalar_one()),
131:            "actor_type": actor_type,
132:            "actor_id": actor_id,
133:            "route": route,
134:            "window_start": window_start,
135:        },

140:def _identify_actor(name: str, request: Request) -> tuple[str, str]:
141:    if name in {"login", "signup"}:
142:        return "ip", _client_ip(request)
143:
144:    if name in {"pairing_initiate", "message_send"}:
145:        return "sender", _required_actor_value(request, "sender_id", "X-Sender-ID")
146:
147:    if name == "message_send_user_hour":
148:        sender_id = _required_actor_value(request, "sender_id", "X-Sender-ID")
149:        user_id = _state_or_request_value(request, "user_id", "X-User-ID")
150:        if user_id is None:
151:            raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST, detail="missing rate limit actor")
152:        return "sender_user", f"{sender_id}:{user_id}"
153:
154:    if name == "manifest_fetch":
155:        return "device", _required_actor_value(request, "device_id", "X-Device-ID")
156:
157:    if name == "action_callback":
158:        return "pairing", _required_actor_value(request, "pairing_id", "X-Pairing-ID")
159:
160:    user_id = getattr(request.state, "user_id", None)
161:    if user_id is not None:
162:        return "user", str(user_id)
163:    return "ip", _client_ip(request)
164:
165:
166:def _required_actor_value(request: Request, path_param: str, header: str) -> str:
167:    value = _state_or_request_value(request, path_param, header)
168:    if value is None:
169:        raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST, detail="missing rate limit actor")
170:    return value
171:
172:
173:def _state_or_request_value(request: Request, path_param: str, header: str) -> str | None:
174:    state_value = getattr(request.state, path_param, None)
175:    if state_value is not None:
176:        return str(state_value)
177:
178:    path_value: Any = request.path_params.get(path_param)
179:    if path_value is not None:
180:        return str(path_value)
181:
182:    header_value = request.headers.get(header)
183:    if header_value:
184:        return header_value
185:
186:    return None
187:

189:def _client_ip(request: Request) -> str:
190:    forwarded_for = request.headers.get("x-forwarded-for")
191:    if forwarded_for:
192:        return forwarded_for.split(",", 1)[0].strip()
193:    if request.client is None:
194:        return "unknown"
195:    return request.client.host

16:    """A sender with this public key is already registered."""

20:    """Sender lookup failed."""

24:    """Sender exists but is revoked."""

26:
27:async def register_sender(
28:    db: AsyncSession,
29:    *,
30:    public_key: bytes,
31:    name: str,
32:    contact: str | None = None,
33:) -> Sender:
34:    sender = Sender(
35:        id=uuid.uuid4(),
36:        public_key=public_key,
37:        name=name,
38:        contact=contact,
39:    )
40:    db.add(sender)
41:    try:
42:        await db.commit()
43:    except IntegrityError as exc:
44:        await db.rollback()
45:        raise SenderAlreadyExistsError("public key already registered") from exc
46:
47:    await db.refresh(sender)
48:    return sender
49:
50:
51:async def get_sender(db: AsyncSession, sender_id: uuid.UUID) -> Sender:
52:    result = await db.execute(select(Sender).where(Sender.id == sender_id))
53:    sender = result.scalar_one_or_none()
54:    if sender is None:
55:        raise SenderNotFoundError(f"sender {sender_id} not found")
56:    return sender
57:
58:
59:async def get_active_sender(db: AsyncSession, sender_id: uuid.UUID) -> Sender:
60:    sender = await get_sender(db, sender_id)
61:    if sender.revoked_at is not None:
62:        raise SenderRevokedError(f"sender {sender_id} is revoked")
63:    return sender
64:
65:
66:async def revoke_sender(db: AsyncSession, sender_id: uuid.UUID) -> Sender:
67:    sender = await get_sender(db, sender_id)
68:    if sender.revoked_at is None:
69:        sender.revoked_at = datetime.now(UTC)
70:        await db.commit()
71:        await db.refresh(sender)
72:    return sender

1:package app.syncler.core.push

16:import kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers
17:import kotlinx.coroutines.Job

19:import kotlinx.coroutines.launch
20:import kotlinx.coroutines.withTimeoutOrNull
21:import timber.log.Timber
22:
23:/**
24: * Foreground service that runs plugin code on FCM wake-up.
25: *
26: * Lifecycle per message:
27: *   1. FCM wakes the app; SynclerFcmService starts this service with metadata.
28: *   2. Service immediately calls startForeground() with a low-priority "Receiving..."
29: *      notification (Android 14+ uses FOREGROUND_SERVICE_TYPE_DATA_SYNC).
30: *   3. PluginMessagePipeline (DI) fetches encrypted body from server, decrypts,
31: *      dispatches to plugin instance's onMessage hook. Plugin returns a
32: *      NotificationDescriptor which becomes the user-visible notification.
33: *   4. Service stops (whether or not the plugin succeeded). 30s hard timeout.
34: */
35:@AndroidEntryPoint
36:class PluginNotificationService : Service() {
37:
38:    @Inject lateinit var pipeline: PluginMessagePipeline
39:    @Inject lateinit var notifications: NotificationFactory
40:
41:    private val scope = CoroutineScope(SupervisorJob() + Dispatchers.IO)
42:    private var workJob: Job? = null
43:
44:    override fun onCreate() {
45:        super.onCreate()
46:        notifications.ensureChannel(this)
47:        startForegroundCompat()
48:    }
49:
50:    override fun onStartCommand(intent: Intent?, flags: Int, startId: Int): Int {
51:        val messageId = intent?.getStringExtra(EXTRA_MESSAGE_ID)
52:        val pluginId = intent?.getStringExtra(EXTRA_PLUGIN_ID)
53:        val minVersion = intent?.getStringExtra(EXTRA_MIN_PLUGIN_VERSION).orEmpty()
54:        if (messageId == null || pluginId == null) {
55:            Timber.tag(TAG).w("missing message_id or plugin_id; stopping")
56:            stopSelf(startId)
57:            return START_NOT_STICKY
58:        }
59:
60:        workJob = scope.launch {
61:            val outcome = withTimeoutOrNull(MAX_WORK_MS) {
62:                pipeline.process(
63:                    messageId = messageId,
64:                    pluginId = pluginId,
65:                    minPluginVersion = minVersion,
66:                )
67:            }
68:            if (outcome == null) {
69:                Timber.tag(TAG).w("plugin pipeline timed out for message=%s", messageId)
70:            } else {
71:                outcome.notification?.let { notifications.post(this@PluginNotificationService, it) }
72:                if (outcome.requiresUpdate) {
73:                    notifications.postUpdateRequired(
74:                        context = this@PluginNotificationService,
75:                        pluginId = pluginId,
76:                        requiredVersion = outcome.requiredVersion ?: minVersion,
77:                    )
78:                }
79:            }
80:            stopSelf(startId)
81:        }
82:        return START_NOT_STICKY
83:    }
84:
85:    override fun onDestroy() {
86:        workJob?.cancel()
87:        super.onDestroy()
88:    }
89:
90:    override fun onBind(intent: Intent?): IBinder? = null
91:
92:    private fun startForegroundCompat() {
93:        val notification: Notification = NotificationCompat.Builder(this, FOREGROUND_CHANNEL_ID)
94:            .setSmallIcon(android.R.drawable.stat_notify_sync)
95:            .setContentTitle("Syncler")
96:            .setContentText("Receiving message…")
97:            .setPriority(NotificationCompat.PRIORITY_LOW)
98:            .setOngoing(true)
99:            .build()
100:        if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.UPSIDE_DOWN_CAKE) {
101:            startForeground(
102:                FOREGROUND_ID,
103:                notification,
104:                ServiceInfo.FOREGROUND_SERVICE_TYPE_DATA_SYNC,
105:            )
106:        } else {
107:            startForeground(FOREGROUND_ID, notification)
108:        }
109:    }
110:
111:    companion object {
112:        private const val TAG = "PluginNotifSvc"
113:        private const val EXTRA_MESSAGE_ID = "syncler.message_id"
114:        private const val EXTRA_PLUGIN_ID = "syncler.plugin_id"
115:        private const val EXTRA_MIN_PLUGIN_VERSION = "syncler.min_plugin_version"
116:
117:        private const val FOREGROUND_ID = 11_001
118:        const val FOREGROUND_CHANNEL_ID = "syncler.foreground.delivery"
119:        const val USER_CHANNEL_ID = "syncler.user.messages"
120:
121:        private const val MAX_WORK_MS = 30_000L
122:
123:        fun start(context: Context, messageId: String, pluginId: String, minPluginVersion: String) {
124:            val intent = Intent(context, PluginNotificationService::class.java).apply {
125:                putExtra(EXTRA_MESSAGE_ID, messageId)
126:                putExtra(EXTRA_PLUGIN_ID, pluginId)
127:                putExtra(EXTRA_MIN_PLUGIN_VERSION, minPluginVersion)
128:            }
129:            if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.O) {
130:                context.startForegroundService(intent)
131:            } else {
132:                context.startService(intent)
133:            }
134:        }
135:    }
136:}
137:
138:/**
139: * Implemented by the host app — fetches encrypted body, decrypts, dispatches
140: * to the loaded plugin instance.
141: */
142:interface PluginMessagePipeline {
143:    suspend fun process(
144:        messageId: String,
145:        pluginId: String,
146:        minPluginVersion: String,
147:    ): PluginMessageOutcome
148:}
149:
150:data class PluginMessageOutcome(
151:    val notification: PluginNotificationRequest? = null,
152:    val requiresUpdate: Boolean = false,
153:    val requiredVersion: String? = null,
154:)
155:
156:data class PluginNotificationRequest(
157:    val title: String,
158:    val body: String,
159:    val importance: String = "default",
160:    val groupId: String? = null,
161:)
162:
163:interface NotificationFactory {
164:    fun ensureChannel(context: Context)
165:    fun post(context: Context, request: PluginNotificationRequest)
166:    fun postUpdateRequired(context: Context, pluginId: String, requiredVersion: String)
167:}
168:
169:class DefaultNotificationFactory @Inject constructor() : NotificationFactory {
170:
171:    override fun ensureChannel(context: Context) {
172:        if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT < Build.VERSION_CODES.O) return
173:        val nm = context.getSystemService(NotificationManager::class.java) ?: return
174:        val foregroundChannel = NotificationChannel(
175:            PluginNotificationService.FOREGROUND_CHANNEL_ID,
176:            "Background delivery",
177:            NotificationManager.IMPORTANCE_MIN,
178:        )
179:        val userChannel = NotificationChannel(
180:            PluginNotificationService.USER_CHANNEL_ID,
181:            "Messages",
182:            NotificationManager.IMPORTANCE_DEFAULT,
183:        )
184:        nm.createNotificationChannel(foregroundChannel)
185:        nm.createNotificationChannel(userChannel)
186:    }
187:
188:    override fun post(context: Context, request: PluginNotificationRequest) {
189:        val nm = context.getSystemService(NotificationManager::class.java) ?: return
190:        val builder = NotificationCompat.Builder(context, PluginNotificationService.USER_CHANNEL_ID)
191:            .setSmallIcon(android.R.drawable.ic_dialog_info)
192:            .setContentTitle(request.title)
193:            .setContentText(request.body)
194:            .setPriority(importanceToPriority(request.importance))
195:            .setAutoCancel(true)
196:        request.groupId?.let { builder.setGroup(it) }
197:        nm.notify(request.hashCode(), builder.build())
198:    }
199:
200:    override fun postUpdateRequired(context: Context, pluginId: String, requiredVersion: String) {
201:        val nm = context.getSystemService(NotificationManager::class.java) ?: return
202:        val builder = NotificationCompat.Builder(context, PluginNotificationService.USER_CHANNEL_ID)
203:            .setSmallIcon(android.R.drawable.stat_sys_warning)
204:            .setContentTitle("Plugin update required")
205:            .setContentText("Tap to update $pluginId to $requiredVersion to view this message")
206:            .setPriority(NotificationCompat.PRIORITY_HIGH)
207:            .setAutoCancel(true)
208:        nm.notify(pluginId.hashCode(), builder.build())
209:    }
210:
211:    private fun importanceToPriority(value: String): Int = when (value) {
212:        "low" -> NotificationCompat.PRIORITY_LOW
213:        "high" -> NotificationCompat.PRIORITY_HIGH
214:        else -> NotificationCompat.PRIORITY_DEFAULT
215:    }
216:}

1:package app.syncler.core.push
2:
3:import android.content.Intent
4:import com.google.firebase.messaging.FirebaseMessagingService
5:import com.google.firebase.messaging.RemoteMessage
6:import dagger.hilt.android.AndroidEntryPoint
7:import javax.inject.Inject
8:import kotlinx.coroutines.CoroutineScope
9:import kotlinx.coroutines.Dispatchers
10:import kotlinx.coroutines.SupervisorJob
11:import kotlinx.coroutines.launch
12:import timber.log.Timber
13:
14:/**
15: * Receives FCM data messages from the Syncler server.
16: *
17: * The payload is intentionally opaque metadata only: `type`, `message_id`,
18: * `plugin_id`, `min_plugin_version`. The service routes by `type` —
19: * `"message"` triggers a foreground service that fetches + decrypts the
20: * encrypted body via [PluginNotificationService]; `"dismiss"` is handled
21: * by [DismissEventHandler].
22: */
23:@AndroidEntryPoint
24:class SynclerFcmService : FirebaseMessagingService() {
25:
26:    @Inject lateinit var dispatcher: FcmDispatcher
27:    @Inject lateinit var fcmTokenRegistrar: FcmTokenRegistrar
28:
29:    private val scope = CoroutineScope(SupervisorJob() + Dispatchers.IO)
30:
31:    override fun onMessageReceived(remoteMessage: RemoteMessage) {
32:        val data = remoteMessage.data
33:        val type = data["type"] ?: run {
34:            Timber.tag(TAG).w("FCM message missing 'type' field; ignoring")
35:            return
36:        }
37:
38:        when (type) {
39:            "message" -> {
40:                val messageId = data["message_id"] ?: return logMissing("message_id")
41:                val pluginId = data["plugin_id"] ?: return logMissing("plugin_id")
42:                val minVersion = data["min_plugin_version"].orEmpty()
43:                PluginNotificationService.start(
44:                    context = applicationContext,
45:                    messageId = messageId,
46:                    pluginId = pluginId,
47:                    minPluginVersion = minVersion,
48:                )
49:            }
50:            "dismiss" -> {
51:                val messageId = data["message_id"] ?: return logMissing("message_id")
52:                val pluginId = data["plugin_id"] ?: return logMissing("plugin_id")
53:                scope.launch {
54:                    dispatcher.dispatchDismiss(messageId, pluginId)
55:                }
56:            }
57:            else -> Timber.tag(TAG).w("unknown FCM payload type: %s", type)
58:        }
59:    }
60:
61:    override fun onNewToken(token: String) {
62:        Timber.tag(TAG).i("new FCM token received")
63:        scope.launch {
64:            runCatching { fcmTokenRegistrar.registerToken(token) }
65:                .onFailure { Timber.tag(TAG).w(it, "failed to register FCM token") }
66:        }
67:    }
68:
69:    private fun logMissing(field: String) {
70:        Timber.tag(TAG).w("FCM data message missing required field: %s", field)
71:    }
72:
73:    companion object {
74:        private const val TAG = "SynclerFcm"
75:    }
76:}
77:
78:/**
79: * Indirection so the service can be unit-tested with a fake.
80: */
81:interface FcmDispatcher {
82:    suspend fun dispatchDismiss(messageId: String, pluginId: String)
83:}
84:
85:interface FcmTokenRegistrar {
86:    suspend fun registerToken(token: String)
87:}

9:/**
10: * Helper used by the host app to detect (and direct the user to disable)
11: * battery optimization. Required on Samsung / OnePlus / many OEMs for
12: * reliable background FCM + foreground-service delivery.
13: *
14: * Usage in the app:
15: *   if (!BatteryOptimizationCheck.isIgnoring(context)) {
16: *       startActivity(BatteryOptimizationCheck.requestIgnoreIntent(context))
17: *   }
18: */
19:object BatteryOptimizationCheck {
20:
21:    fun isIgnoring(context: Context): Boolean {
22:        val pm = context.getSystemService(Context.POWER_SERVICE) as? PowerManager ?: return false
23:        return pm.isIgnoringBatteryOptimizations(context.packageName)
24:    }
25:
26:    fun requestIgnoreIntent(context: Context): Intent =
27:        Intent(Settings.ACTION_REQUEST_IGNORE_BATTERY_OPTIMIZATIONS)
28:            .setData(Uri.parse("package:${context.packageName}"))
29:            .addFlags(Intent.FLAG_ACTIVITY_NEW_TASK)
30:}

1:"""AES-256-GCM helpers and canonical AAD assembly."""
2:
3:from __future__ import annotations
4:
5:import json
6:from typing import Any, Final
7:
8:from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.ciphers.aead import AESGCM
9:
10:AES_256_KEY_BYTES: Final[int] = 32
11:AES_GCM_NONCE_BYTES: Final[int] = 12
12:AES_GCM_TAG_BYTES: Final[int] = 16
13:
14:AAD_REQUIRED_FIELDS: Final[tuple[str, ...]] = (
15:    "message_id",
16:    "sender_id",
17:    "user_id",
18:    "plugin_id",
19:    "min_plugin_version",
20:    "created_at",
21:    "schema_version",
22:)
23:AAD_REQUIRED_FIELD_SET: Final[frozenset[str]] = frozenset(AAD_REQUIRED_FIELDS)
24:
25:
26:def decrypt_message_body(pairing_key: bytes, wire: bytes, aad: bytes) -> bytes:
27:    """Decrypt a packed AES-GCM message body."""
28:
29:    if len(pairing_key) != AES_256_KEY_BYTES:
30:        raise ValueError("pairing_key must be 32 bytes")
31:    if len(wire) < AES_GCM_NONCE_BYTES + AES_GCM_TAG_BYTES:
32:        raise ValueError("wire is too short")
33:
34:    nonce = wire[:AES_GCM_NONCE_BYTES]
35:    ciphertext_with_tag = wire[AES_GCM_NONCE_BYTES:]
36:    return AESGCM(pairing_key).decrypt(nonce, ciphertext_with_tag, aad)
37:
38:
39:def assemble_aad(fields: dict[str, Any]) -> bytes:
40:    """Assemble canonical JSON AAD for message encryption."""
41:
42:    missing_fields = [field for field in AAD_REQUIRED_FIELDS if field not in fields]
43:    if missing_fields:
44:        raise ValueError(f"missing AAD fields: {', '.join(missing_fields)}")
45:
46:    unexpected_fields = sorted(set(fields) - AAD_REQUIRED_FIELD_SET)
47:    if unexpected_fields:
48:        raise ValueError(f"unexpected AAD fields: {', '.join(unexpected_fields)}")
49:
50:    return json.dumps(
51:        fields,
52:        ensure_ascii=True,
53:        separators=(",", ":"),
54:        sort_keys=True,
55:    ).encode("utf-8")

1:package app.syncler.core.crypto
2:
3:data class MessageAad(
4:    val messageId: String,
5:    val senderId: String,
6:    val userId: String,
7:    val pluginId: String,
8:    val minPluginVersion: Int,
9:    val createdAt: String,
10:    val schemaVersion: Int,
11:)
12:
13:fun MessageAad.toCanonicalJsonBytes(): ByteArray {
14:    val fields = mapOf(
15:        "created_at" to createdAt,
16:        "message_id" to messageId,
17:        "min_plugin_version" to minPluginVersion,
18:        "plugin_id" to pluginId,
19:        "schema_version" to schemaVersion,
20:        "sender_id" to senderId,
21:        "user_id" to userId,
22:    )
23:    return canonicalJsonBytes(fields)
24:}
25:
26:internal fun canonicalJsonBytes(fields: Map<String, Any>): ByteArray =
27:    fields.entries.sortedBy { it.key }.joinToString(prefix = "{", postfix = "}", separator = ",") { (key, value) ->
28:        val encodedValue = when (value) {
29:            is Int -> value.toString()
30:            is String -> "\"${value.jsonEscape()}\""
31:            else -> error("unsupported AAD value")
32:        }
33:        "\"$key\":$encodedValue"
34:    }.encodeToByteArray()
35:
36:private fun String.jsonEscape(): String = buildString {
37:    for (char in this@jsonEscape) {
38:        when (char) {
39:            '\\' -> append("\\\\")
40:            '"' -> append("\\\"")
41:            '\b' -> append("\\b")
42:            '\u000C' -> append("\\f")
43:            '\n' -> append("\\n")
44:            '\r' -> append("\\r")
45:            '\t' -> append("\\t")
46:            else -> if (char.code < 0x20 || char.code > 0x7E) {
47:                append("\\u%04x".format(char.code))
48:            } else {
49:                append(char)
50:            }
51:        }
52:    }
53:}

.triad\01-claude-vote.md:14:The idea has a sharp wedge wrapped in a vague platform. The wedge — "my agent needs me but I'm not at my desk, send the prompt to my phone with proper UI" — is real, immediate, and the user is themselves the first customer. The platform vision (Alpaca, KYC, any service to any human) is a true endgame but a fantasy V1 — it requires two-sided adoption that nothing in the plan addresses. The prior Claude got the diagnosis right: scope is the central risk, timeline is the second. The thing nobody has pressed yet is **what counts as "done."** The user said "kill it" but didn't define a single observable outcome — no "X users", no "Y daily sessions", no "Z senders integrated." Without that, scope can't be cut, because cutting requires knowing what to cut toward. That's the first question I'd ask.

.triad\05-triad-vote.md:6:- Q19: V1 = sideload/URL install (user is only user). Marketplace required before public ship → V1.5.
.triad\05-triad-vote.md:8:- Q24: AWS free tier for V1. Plan transition before ship.
.triad\05-triad-vote.md:21:**Reason:** Sender publishes a QR encoding `{ plugin_manifest_url, one_time_pairing_token, sender_public_key_fingerprint }`. User scans with their phone app → app fetches the manifest → verifies signature → shows install confirmation with declared capabilities → user taps install → app generates user keypair, exchanges with sender's server via the one-time token → pairing done. Why QR over URL-paste: (a) phone is already in hand, (b) one-time token can be short-lived and embedded, (c) prevents typo-domain phishing. URL-paste (option b from user's choices) is a fine fallback for headless contexts but QR is the V1 default.
.triad\05-triad-vote.md:23:### Q17 — Server SDK language: **Python V1, JS/TS V1.1, curl-friendly docs from day 1**
.triad\05-triad-vote.md:24:**Reason:** Both of user's concrete senders (trading bot, lottery app) are Python-friendly. The lottery's Claude Code dogfood test happens in Python world. Building two SDKs in parallel doubles the surface to maintain and doesn't unlock anything user has actually committed to. Curl examples cover Node/Go/Rust senders for "make it work" at zero cost. Add JS/TS in V1.1 when there's a JS sender that matters.
.triad\05-triad-vote.md:26:### Q23 — Plugin updates: **Prompt-to-update for V1 (URL install era), auto-update with marketplace re-review gate for V1.5**
.triad\05-triad-vote.md:27:**Reason:** In V1, plugins are installed by URL — no review gate catches a malicious update. Auto-update would let a compromised sender push code to user's phone silently. Prompt-to-update is one tap; user is the only user; not annoying. When marketplace ships V1.5, re-review on each version becomes the trust anchor, and auto-update is safe again.

.triad\06-codex-log.txt:108:devices; V1 needs account-level message IDs and sender-side idempotency so two phones cannot accidentally submit the 
.triad\06-codex-log.txt:127:The zero-knowledge multi-device model is sound, but the key hierarchy needs to be explicit: password-derived key unlocks an encrypted user master key; sender pairings and message keys hang off that, not directly off the password. Broker pairing fits multi-device if pairing attaches to the user account/master public identity, then syncs encrypted sender state to every device. `platform.showNotification(...)` creates duplicate notification and action risks across devices; V1 needs account-level message IDs and sender-side idempotency so two phones cannot accidentally submit the same action twice. Plugin version pinning still works, but every device must be able to fetch/cache the exact plugin version required to render or handle a message.
.triad\06-codex-out.txt:2:The zero-knowledge multi-device model is sound, but the key hierarchy needs to be explicit: password-derived key unlocks an encrypted user master key; sender pairings and message keys hang off that, not directly off the password. .triad\08-codex-log.txt:1007:# Syncler V1 - Build Plan (Final, arbitrated by Codex)
.triad\08-codex-log.txt:1009:Working name: **Syncler**. Final naming is deferred to V1.5.
.triad\08-codex-log.txt:1011:V1 is a multi-device, end-to-end encrypted, plugin-host platform. External programs push structured messages to a user’s Android phone or phones. Each sender ships a signed JavaScript plugin defining its data, UI, notifications, and actions. The platform brokers identity, delivery, pairing, revocation, update checks, and encrypted state sync while remaining content-blind.
.triad\08-codex-log.txt:1015:**V1 stack:** Python FastAPI server, PostgreSQL, AWS free-tier-compatible deployment path, Kotlin Jetpack Compose Android app, Android WebView plugin host, JavaScript plugin SDK, Python sender SDK.
.triad\08-codex-log.txt:1021:**V1 demo target:** trading bot and lottery plugin both function end-to-end. The lottery plugin is still used as the developer-experience dogfood test, but the deliverable is a DX issue report plus integration result, not a theatrical pass/fail claim.

.triad\27-review-m5-prompt.md:33:1. **Envelope canonical bytes.** `routers/messages.py` builds `envelope_bytes` from `{sender_id, user_id, plugin_id, encrypted_body, nonce, min_plugin_version}` with sort_keys + separators(",", ":"). Sender SDK (not yet written — M9) MUST produce byte-identical bytes when signing. Is the field set complete? Should `expires_at` or a server-generated `message_id` be in the AAD/envelope? Trade-off: more fields = more replay protection, fewer fields = sender doesn't need to predict server state.
.triad\27-review-m5-prompt.md:35:2. **AAD vs envelope.** The crypto-spec defines AAD = (message_id, sender_id, user_id, plugin_id, min_plugin_version, created_at, schema_version). But message_id is server-generated AFTER the sender signs. How does the sender include message_id in AAD if they don't know it yet? Either the AAD must be relaxed for V1 OR the sender generates a client-side message_id and the server adopts it. Currently the schema_version + created_at + message_id fields are likely DROPPED in my impl. Check.
.triad\27-review-m5-prompt.md:47:8. **Battery optimization UX.** `BatteryOptimizationCheck.requestIgnoreIntent` opens system settings. The Android manifest doesn't declare the related permission (`REQUEST_IGNORE_BATTERY_OPTIMIZATIONS`) — Play Store has policy restrictions on apps that request this. Is the helper enough for V1 (where user is dev) or does it need policy doc?
.triad\27-review-m5-prompt.md:49:9. **POST /send rate limit by sender_id from header X-Sender-ID.** Header is unauthenticated input before signature verification. A spammer could send a flood of requests with random X-Sender-ID values bypassing the per-sender bucket. Counter-argument: each request still has to hit signature verification which is CPU-bound, but the bucket itself can be flooded. Is this OK for V1 or do we move to IP rate limit?
.triad\27-gemini-review.txt:7:- **1. Envelope canonical bytes:** Concur. `expires_at` is part of the request but not the signed envelope, allowing an attacker to replay a message long after its intended expiry. It should be added to the envelope.

=== AGREEMENTS WITH CLAUDE'S SELF-FLAGGED ITEMS ===
1. **#1** - Concur. Envelope fields are not complete if `expires_at` is sender-controlled; do not add server-generated `message_id` unless sender supplies it.
2. **#2** - Concur hard. Current M5 violates the crypto AAD contract: `message_id`, `created_at`, and `schema_version` are required by spec but cannot be known by the sender under current flow.
3. **#3** - Concur, but not acceptable as-is. `docs/crypto-spec.md:196` says V1 does in-memory per-sender replay checks; `/send` does not call `NonceRegistry`.
4. **#4** - Mostly safe. `|` is not in base64; parser should still use `validate=True` and length checks for DB-corruption robustness.
5. **#5** - Confirmed. FCM payload only includes `type`, `message_id`, `plugin_id`, `min_plugin_version`; no plaintext path found.
6. **#6** - Partly concur. 30s is a reasonable ceiling, but silent timeout is bad UX; emit a generic failure/retry notification or durable retry event.
7. **#7** - Concur. Foreground delivery and user-message channels should be separate.
8. **#8** - Concur. Helper is not enough for production: either add `REQUEST_IGNORE_BATTERY_OPTIMIZATIONS` plus policy justification, or use a general settings intent for V1 dev builds.
9. **#9** - Concur. Pre-auth `/send` needs IP/global limiting; verified sender limiting can happen after signature verification.
10. **#10** - Concur. Add `device_id` ownership validation; own-account scope, but current behavior can mark/push using another device id.

=== ADDITIONAL FINDINGS ===
- **high** Sender can send using another sender's plugin id  
  evidence: `server/app/services/messages.py:59`, `server/app/services/messages.py:80`, `server/app/models.py:87`  
  proposal: fetch plugin with `Plugin.id == plugin_id AND Plugin.sender_id == sender_id AND revoked_at IS NULL`.

- **high** Android app likely does not compile due missing Hilt bindings  
  evidence: `android/app/build.gradle.kts:42`, `android/core/push/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/core/push/SynclerFcmService.kt:26`, `android/core/push/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/core/push/PluginNotificationService.kt:38`, `android/core/push/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/core/push/PushModule.kt:13`  
  proposal: land app-level bindings/stubs for `PluginMessagePipeline`, `FcmDispatcher`, and `FcmTokenRegistrar`, or do not include `:core:push` in the app until host implementations exist.

- **high** `/send` can succeed with no reachable push target  
  evidence: `server/app/services/messages.py:37`, `server/app/services/messages.py:84`, `server/app/services/push.py:78`, `server/app/services/push.py:86`  
  proposal: treat “no active non-revoked device with `fcm_token`” as 410, or explicitly document inbox-only delivery.

- **medium** Expired messages can be accepted and fetched until retention runs  
  evidence: `server/app/schemas.py:141`, `server/app/services/messages.py:88`, `server/app/services/messages.py:102`, `server/app/services/messages.py:143`  
  proposal: reject past `expires_at`, cap max expiry, include it in signed envelope if sender-controlled, and filter expired rows in inbox/get.

- **medium** Rapid FCM starts can orphan plugin work  
  evidence: `android/core/push/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/core/push/PluginNotificationService.kt:41`, `:42`, `:60`, `:85`  
  proposal: track all jobs or serialize through a queue; cancel the whole service scope on destroy, not only the latest `workJob`.

- **medium** Dismiss/token async work is fire-and-forget from `FirebaseMessagingService`  
  evidence: `android/core/push/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/core/push/SynclerFcmService.kt:29`, `:53`, `:63`  
  proposal: use WorkManager or another durable bounded handoff for dismiss and token registration.

=== SHOW-STOPPERS ===
AAD/message-id contract mismatch; missing replay check; plugin ownership check; Android missing Hilt bindings; `/send` success with no reachable FCM token.

=== SAFE / NOT-AN-ISSUE ===
FCM plaintext leakage: ruled out.

Inline pointer separator: safe against malicious base64 `|`; harden parser but not a blocker.

Notification channel split: right design.

30s service budget: acceptable ceiling, but needs failure surface.

Server-generated `message_id` should not be added to sender envelope unless M5 changes to client-generated ids.
